# Heartland Dental Paid Media - Synthetic Dataset

This document contains all synthetic media performance data for Heartland Dental offices.
Data covers the period from January 2023 through December 2024 across 10 dental offices and 3 media channels (Google Search, Meta, Google Programmatic).

---

## 1. Data Dictionary and Overview

Heartland Dental — Synthetic Paid Media Datas,,
SYNTHETIC DATA — FOR DEMO PURPOSES ONLY | 10 Offices | 3 Channels | 2 Years Week,,
,,
SHEETS IN THIS WORKBOOK,,
Weekly_Raw_Data,Weekly grain — all 10 offices × 3 channels × 104 weeks. Primary data,
Monthly_Summary,"Monthly rollup of spend, conversions, CPA, bookings by office and channel.",
Office_Summary,Full 2-year totals and averages by office and channel. Good for portfolio view.,
Office_Profiles,"Office metadata: market size, maturity, capacity profile, and channel mix assumptions.",
,,
,,
FIELD DICTIONARY — WEEKLY_RAW_DA,,
Week_Start,Date of Monday starting each week (ISO week),
Week_Year / Week_Num,Year and ISO week number for easy slicing,
OfficeID,Heartland office identifier (matches OfficeMetaData.xlsx),
OfficeName / City / State,Office display name and location,
Channel,Google_Search | Meta | Google_Programmatic,
Spend,Total paid media spend ($) for the week on this channel,
Impressions,Total ad impressions served,
Clicks,Total clicks on ads,
CTR,Click-through rate = Clicks / Impressions,
CPC,Cost per click = Spend / Clicks,
Conversions_Observed,Conversions platform-reported (includes non-incremental credit),
Conversions_Incremental,True incremental conversions — patients who would NOT have booked without the ,
Incrementality_Rate,"Conversions_Incremental / Conversions_Observed (Meta ~63%, Google Search ~82%, Prog ~74%)",
CPA_Observed,Cost per acquisition using platform-reported conversions,
CPA_Incremental,True CPA using only incremental conversions — KEY METRIC for optimizati,
New_Patient_Bookings,Estimated new patient appointments booked (subset of observed conversions),
Attributed_Revenue,Revenue proxy ($) at ~$380 avg first-visit patient value,
Capacity_Utilization,Office appointment capacity used that week (0–1). Constrains realistic lif,
Seasonality_Factor,"Dental seasonality multiplier applied (Q1 peak, summer dip)",
,,
